I want to say one thing and this is NOT to defend dream. Dream has ADHD. And at that unmedicated ADHD. As someone who has ADHD and is now medicated again for roughly a year after 19 years of my life without meds (long story short, my mom thought the meds would get me hooked even tho thats impossible for adhd havers and I even flat out forgot for several years that I had ADHD), this stuff can mess with your brain EXTREMELY.  Whats going on right now isnt narcisism. Whats going on right now is basically a drug trip. He gets serotonin from what makes him happy, just that what makes him happy is interacting with his fans in funny and sometimes very odd ways. It comes to the point where his impulsivity takes over more than anything and he ends up doing crap that he really shouldnt. I say this as an ADHD haver who has been very stupid sometimes similar to him. NOT TO THE EXTENT MIND but that is also because I had my mother around who took care of me for the most part. DREAM DOES NOT.  Dream, right now is basically in this state of mind where he feels younger than he is. He feels like a kid so he acts like a kid. No Im not making this crap up. ADHD can seriously mess with your brain if you dont take fricking meds!  So what is this comment about specifically? Mainly countering the accusations of him being narcissistic. Thats it. Thats all there is to it. My problem is not that people think he is that, my problem is that I have been called that as well and only later learned more about adhd where I could counteract it personally. This November, when the fight with Cantu was happening, a new Anonymous account appeared that showed screenshots of a conversation from 2019 in which a girl called Jamie sent someone else the videos. Lettuce (Lactuca sativa) is an annual plant of the family Asteraceae. It is most often grown as a leaf vegetable, but sometimes for its stem and seeds. Lettuce is most often used for salads, although it is also seen in other kinds of food, such as soups, sandwiches and wraps; it can also be grilled.[3] One variety, celtuce (asparagus lettuce), is grown for its stems, which are eaten either raw or cooked. In addition to its main use as a leafy green, it has also gathered religious and medicinal significance over centuries of human consumption. Europe and North America originally dominated the market for lettuce, but by the late 20th century the consumption of lettuce had spread throughout the world. As of 2021, world production of lettuce and chicory was 27 million tonnes, 53 percent of which came from China.[4]
